`health_checker_impl.cc`.\\n\\n## Primary Implementation\\n\\nThe **GrpcHealthCheckerFactory** class in `health_checker_impl.h` implements the `CustomHealthCheckerFactory` interface and is registered with the name \\\"envoy.health_checkers.grpc\\\". The factory's `createCustomHealthChecker()` method is called by the `HealthCheckerFactory::create()` method in `source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.cc` when a gRPC health check configuration is detected (via the `kGrpcHealthCheck` case in the health check type switch statement).\\n\\nThe **GrpcHealthCheckerImpl** class extends `HealthCheckerImplBase` and manages the overall gRPC health checking behavior. It contains a nested **GrpcActiveHealthCheckSession** class that implements the actual protocol interaction:\\n\\n### HealthCheckRequest Handling\\nThe `onInterval()` method in `GrpcActiveHealthCheckSession` sends a `grpc::health::v1::HealthCheckRequest` to the target service. It:\\n1. Creates an HTTP/2 connection using `parent_.createCodecClient()`\\n2. Prepares gRPC request headers for the `grpc.health.v1.Health/Check` method\\n3. Serializes and sends the HealthCheckRequest message with optional service name parameter\\n\\n### HealthCheckResponse Parsing\\nThe response handling is distributed across three methods:\\n- **decodeData()**: Deserializes the gRPC frame containing `grpc::health::v1::HealthCheckResponse` using protobuf parsing\\n- **decodeHeaders()**: Validates the HTTP/2 response status and gRPC metadata\\n- **decodeTrailers()**: Extracts the gRPC status code from response trailers\\n\\n### Health Status Mapping\\nThe **isHealthCheckSucceeded()** method evaluates the response:\\n- Requires gRPC status code to be `Ok` (0)\\n- Checks that `HealthCheckResponse.status()` equals `SERVING` (1)\\n- Returns false for any other status including `NOT_SERVING` (2), `UNKNOWN` (0), and `SERVICE_UNKNOWN` (3)\\n\\nThe **logHealthCheckStatus()** method maps response statuses to human-readable labels:\\n- `SERVING` → \\\"serving\\\" (healthy)\\n- `NOT_SERVING` → \\\"not_serving\\\" (unhealthy)\\n- `UNKNOWN` → \\\"unknown\\\" (treated as unhealthy)\\n- `SERVICE_UNKNOWN` → \\\"service_unknown\\\" (unhealthy)\\n- RPC errors → \\\"rpc_error\\\"\\n\\n## Configuration Schema\\nThe gRPC health check configuration is defined in `api/envoy/config/core/v3/health_check.proto` with the `GrpcHealthCheck` message type that supports:\\n- `service_name`: Optional parameter sent in HealthCheckRequest\\n- `authority`: Overrides the default :authority header value\\n- `initial_metadata`: Custom key-value pairs added to gRPC request headers\\n\\n## Supporting Infrastructure\\nThe implementation relies on:\\n- **source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.h/cc**: Factory pattern registration and health check routing logic\\n- **source/extensions/health_checkers/common/health_checker_base_impl.h/cc**: Base class providing timing, callbacks, and host status management\\n- **src/proto/grpc/health/v1/health.pb.h**: Protocol buffer definitions for the standard gRPC health check service messages\\n\\nThe factory is registered via `REGISTER_FACTORY(GrpcHealthCheckerFactory, Server::Configuration::CustomHealthCheckerFactory)` in health_checker_impl.cc, making it available for automatic instantiation when a cluster's health check configuration includes the gRPC health (unhealthy)\\n- `UNKNOWN` → \\\"unknown\\\" (treated as unhealthy)\\n- `SERVICE_UNKNOWN` → \\\"service_unknown\\\" (unhealthy)\\n- RPC errors → \\\"rpc_error\\\"\\n\\n## Configuration Schema\\nThe gRPC health check configuration is defined in `api/envoy/config/core/v3/health_check.proto` with the `GrpcHealthCheck` message type that supports:\\n- `service_name`: Optional parameter sent in HealthCheckRequest\\n- `authority`: Overrides the default :authority header value\\n- `initial_metadata`: Custom key-value pairs added to gRPC request headers\\n\\n## Supporting Infrastructure\\nThe implementation relies on:\\n- **source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.h/cc**: Factory pattern registration and health check routing logic\\n- **source/extensions/health_checkers/common/health_checker_base_impl.h/cc**: Base class providing timing, callbacks, and host status management\\n- **src/proto/grpc/health/v1/health.pb.h**: Protocol buffer definitions for the standard gRPC health check service messages\\n\\nThe factory is registered via `REGISTER_FACTORY(GrpcHealthCheckerFactory, Server::Configuration::CustomHealthCheckerFactory)` in health_checker_impl.cc, making it available for automatic instantiation when a cluster's health check configuration includes the gRPC health check type.\"\n}\n","numLines":133,"startLine":1,"totalLines":133}}}
